# <a name="release-notes-for-office-current-channel-preview"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-103">Office 版本資訊目前通道 (預覽)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-103">Release Notes for Office Current Channel (Preview)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5bc52-p101">This article contains release notes for Current Channel (Preview) builds of Word, Excel, PowerPoint, Outlook, Access, and Project for Windows desktop. Every week, we’ll highlight interesting new features, important fixes, and any significant issues we want you to know about. Note that we often roll out features (and sometimes even fixes) to Current Channel (Preview) over a period of time. This allows us to ensure that things are working smoothly before releasing the feature to a wider audience. So, if you don’t see something described below, don't worry you'll get it eventually.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-p101">This article contains release notes for Current Channel (Preview) builds of Word, Excel, PowerPoint, Outlook, Access, and Project for Windows desktop. Every week, we’ll highlight interesting new features, important fixes, and any significant issues we want you to know about. Note that we often roll out features (and sometimes even fixes) to Current Channel (Preview) over a period of time. This allows us to ensure that things are working smoothly before releasing the feature to a wider audience. So, if you don’t see something described below, don't worry you'll get it eventually.</span></span>  

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-p102">We’re making some changes to the update channels for Microsoft 365 Apps, including adding a new update channel (Monthly Enterprise Channel) and changing the names of the existing update channels. To learn more, [read this article](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2127441).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-p102">We’re making some changes to the update channels for Microsoft 365 Apps, including adding a new update channel (Monthly Enterprise Channel) and changing the names of the existing update channels. To learn more, [read this article](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2127441).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-111">版本資訊發佈日期可能與實際組建發行日期不相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-111">The release notes publication date may not match the actual build release date.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-131">我們新增了一個 RegKey，可讓客戶停用 IDataObject 操作 (例如，拖曳拖放、剪貼簿) 中附件的 FileTime 包含。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-131">We added a regkey that allows customers to disable filetime inclusion for attachments in IDataObject operations (i.e. drag drop, clipboard).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-132">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Attachments.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-132">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Attachments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-133">REG_DWORD IncludeFileTimesInDataObject.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-133">REG_DWORD IncludeFileTimesInDataObject.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-134">0 = 不包含 filetimes。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-134">0 = filetimes are excluded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-135">1 = (預設) 包含 filetimes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-135">1 = (default) filetimes are included</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-136">我們修正了當回復含有「Azure 資訊保護」保護標籤的郵件時，會導致內嵌影像消失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-136">We fixed an issue that caused inline images to disappear when replying to a message with a protection label from Azure Information Protection.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-164">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-164">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-165">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-165">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-166">修正某些使用者在嘗試從其同步處理的 OneDrive 資料夾匯出査詢時看到「系統資源滿載」錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-166">We fixed an issue where some users were seeing the "system resource exceeded" error when they tried to export a query from their synced OneDrive folder.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-167">我們已修正表單視窗之間發生「自動」切換而切換到另一個表單的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-167">We fixed an issue where 'auto'-switching between form windows was switching to another form.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-168">我們已修正從非 Office 應用程式使用 DAO 時，會導致應用程式意外關閉的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-168">We fixed an issue when using DAO from non-Office applications would cause the application to close unexpectedly.</span></span>


### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-169">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-169">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-170">我們已修正啟用 SaveAs 作業與 COM 增益集之後，檔案名稱未變更的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-170">We fixed an issue where Filename was not changing after a SaveAs operation with COM add-ins enabled.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-171">修正 Power Pivot 使用 Oracle 資料庫連線時的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-171">Fixed an issue with Power Pivot when using a connection to an Oracle database.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-172">我們已修正當 Excel 資料模型中有錯誤的度量定義時，自動儲存會失敗且顯示錯誤/令人誤解的錯誤訊息的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-172">We fixed an issue when Auto-Save fails with incorrect/misleading error message when there's a bad measure definition in the Excel data model.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-173">我們已修正觸發 MTR 計算和群組原則物件更新 (例如，透過遠端群組原則重新整理) 的處理序時，Excel 異常終止的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-173">We fixed an issue where Excel terminated unexpectedly when the process of MTR calc and Group Policy Object update (e.g. via Remote Group Policy Refresh) was triggered.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-174">我們已修正使用者無法直接從 SharePoint 開啟 atomsvc (UTF8+BOM) 檔案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-174">We fixed an issue where a user was unable to open atomsvc (UTF8+BOM) file from SharePoint, directly.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-175">我們已修正放大和縮小簡報區域會造成縮放的選取跑馬燈和滑鼠指標之間產生間隙的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-175">We fixed an issue where zooming in and out from the presentation area resulted in a gap between the zoomed selection marquee and the mouse pointer.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-176">我們已修正將 Excel 活頁簿插入 Word 文件時，Word 似乎停止回應的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-176">We fixed an issue where Word appears to hang when inserting an Excel workbook into a Word document.</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-177">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-177">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-178">解決在新增或儲存附件時，會導致 Outlook 偶爾停止運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-178">Addressed an issue which caused Outlook to stop working sporadically when adding or saving attachments.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-179">我們已修正快速列印影像附件導致錯誤的問題，錯誤為：「Windows 找不到此圖片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-179">We fixed an issue where quick print for image attachments resulted in error, "Windows can't find this picture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-180">請檢查位置，然後再試一次」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-180">Check the location, and then try again".</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-181">我們已修正導致某些使用者看到 Outlook 在離線狀態下啟動，直到他們手動選擇線上工作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-181">We fixed an issue that caused some users to see Outlook start in an Offline state until they manually chose to work online.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-182">我們已修正將從會議位置複製的 URL 貼上到其他位置 (例如瀏覽器) 時，URL 的結尾會包含分號的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-182">We fixed an issue when pasting a URL copied from meeting location to somewhere else (such as a browser), the URL contains a semicolon at the end.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-183">我們已修正使用者無法在 [基本驗證] 中刪除 Microsoft 365 群組行事曆約會的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-183">We fixed an issue where users were unable to delete appointments in Calendar of Microsoft 365 Groups in Basic Auth.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-184">我們已修正載入暱稱快取時啟動 Outlook 失敗的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-184">We fixed an issue where starting Outlook failed while loading nickname cache.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-185">我們已修正信箱擁有者無法管理自己行事曆的共用權限的問題，因為該選項呈現灰色停用狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-185">We fixed an issue where a mailbox owner wasn't able to manage Shared permission for their own Calendar as the option was greyed out.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-186">我們已修正 Outlook 無法使用受限制的權限建立郵件的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-186">We fixed an issue where Outlook was not able to create a message with restricted permission.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-187">我們已修正將電子郵件範本儲存為 .OFT 時，會將中文字元變更為問號的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-187">We fixed an issue where saving email templates as .OFT changed Chinese characters to question marks.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-195">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-195">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-196">已修正如果 [工作表單] 類型檢視中的延遲變更，ProjectBeforeTaskChagne 事件中的 NewVal 值不正確的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-196">Fixed an issue where the NewVal in the ProjectBeforeTaskChagne event doesn't have the correct value if a lag is changed within a Task Form type view.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-197">我們已修正在開啟以特定方式指定資源分佈的檔案時，Project 可能會意外終止的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-197">Fixed an issue where Project may terminate unexpectedly on opening files where resource contours were specified in a certain manner.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-198">已修正當您將專案從 PWA 儲存到本機 mpp 檔案時，會針對實際上使用者未變更的資料觸發 ProjectBeforeTaskChangeEvent 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-198">Fixed an issue where when you save a project from PWA to a local mpp file, the ProjectBeforeTaskChangeEvent fires for data that wasn't actually changed by the user.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-199">已修正資源預訂依名稱 (而不是 GUID) 搜尋資源時，如果有多個名稱相同的資源，會導致問題的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-199">Fixed an issue where resource engagements searched for a resource by name instead of GUID which would cause issues if there were multiple resources with the same name.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-200">已修正如果您在專案網站中有工作清單並將工作清單分組，您將無法快速編輯工作清單的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-200">Fixed an issue where if you have a task list in a project site and group the task list, you will not be able to quick edit the task list.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-201">已修正如果您透過 CSOM 更新企業資源，可能會遺失資源最大單位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-201">Fixed an issue where if you update an enterprise resource via CSOM, resource max units may be lost.</span></span>


### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-202">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-202">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-203">我們已修正放大和縮小簡報區域會造成縮放的選取跑馬燈和滑鼠指標之間產生間隙的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-203">We fixed an issue where zooming in and out from the presentation area resulted in a gap between the zoomed selection marquee and the mouse pointer.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-204">我們已修正按一下註解提示時，註解提示不會放大以在檢視中顯示註解卡片的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-204">We fixed an issue where clicking comment hint didn't zoom out to show comment card in view.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-205">我們已修正欄位之間的線條可能已移位的版面配置問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-205">We fixed a layout issue which the line between columns might have shifted.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-206">我們已修正有時開啟 Word 文件可能會顯示錯誤對話方塊的追蹤修訂問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-206">We fixed an issue in Track Changes which sometimes opening Word document might display error dialog.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-207">我們已修正將 Excel 活頁簿插入 Word 文件時，Word 似乎停止回應的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-207">We fixed an issue where Word appears to hang when inserting an Excel workbook into a Word document.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-208">我們已修正套用具有浮水印的敏感度標籤時的列印問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-208">We fixed a print issue when sensitivity label with watermarks are applied.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-309">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-309">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-310">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-310">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-311">我們已修正載入儲存的查詢/關聯視窗在捲動時，捲軸位置未正確設定的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-311">We fixed an issue where scrollbar position was not set correctly when loading query/relationship window saved while scrolled.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-312">我們已修正 [新增表格] 工作窗格未正確顯示包含 '&' 名稱的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-312">We fixed an issue where Add Table Task Pane was not displaying names containing '&' correctly.</span></span>


### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-313">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-313">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-314">我們已修正多層次類別的手動間隔在圖表中無法運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-314">We fixed an issue where multi-level category manual interval was not working in charts.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-315">修正在使用 2D 地圖圖表時，無法使用 VBA 設定系列中最大值、中間值和最小值顏色的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-315">Fixed an issue with 2D Map Charts where using VBA to set the colors for the max, mid, and min values for a series was not working.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-316">修正可能會導致「嘗試計算一個或多個公式時，Excel 資源不足」的錯誤問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-316">Fixed an issue which could cause an error that "Excel ran out of resources while attempting to calculate one or more formulas".</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-317">修正當 Office 語言設定為西班牙文時，其中資料驗證清單可能無法顯示清單中所有項目的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-317">Fixed an issue when the Office language was set to Spanish, in which data validation lists may not show all the items in the list.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-318">修正在啟用「分頁預覽」時，在含有大量資料的工作表之間切換時，可能會發生明顯延遲的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-318">Fixed an issue where there could be a noticeable delay when switching between worksheets with large amounts of data when 'Page Break Preview' was enabled.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-319">我們已修正當新增至用於資料驗證的表格時，並未更新活頁簿中所有工作表選項的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-319">We fixed an issue where adding to a table used for Data Validation did not update options for all sheets in the workbook.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-320">我們已修正在重新整理 OLAP 樞紐分析表時，可能會導致當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-320">We fixed an issue which could cause a hang when refreshing OLAP PivotTables.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-321">已修正在使用資料編輯列輸入公式時，某些情況下 ChartSheet 出現當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-321">Fixed an issue where ChartSheet crashed in some cases when a formula is entered through formula bar.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-322">我們修正了 Excel 公式列與設備失去連線後無法完全呈現的問題，例如遠端會話的連線/斷線或監視器變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-322">We fixed an issue where the Excel formula bar would not render completely after connection to a device was lost, such as a remote session connect/disconnect or a monitor change.</span></span>


### <a name="onenote"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-323">OneNote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-323">OneNote</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-324">我們修正了使用者無法從 [外部空間檔案] > [資訊] 的文字方塊中選取及複製筆記本 URL 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-324">We fixed an issue where a user was unable to select and copy notebook URL from textbox in OutSpace File > Info.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-325">我們已修正當您將游標移至筆記本色彩選擇器的綠色上方時，快顯會顯示「紅粉色」的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-325">We fixed an issue when you hover over green color in notebook color selector, the pop up reads "red chalk".</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-326">我們已修正 OneNote 在自訂主題的畫布中不會採用高對比色彩的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-326">We fixed an issue where OneNote didn't honor High Contrast colors in the canvas for custom themes.</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-327">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-327">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-328">已解決當主旨為空白時，會導致傳送的自動產生電子郵件含有空白內文的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-328">Addresses an issue that caused automatically generated emails to be sent with a blank body when the subject is blank.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-329">我們修正了資料夾中快取錯誤資料夾 guid 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-329">We fixed an issue where the wrong folder guid is cached for folders.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-330">當使用者將電子郵件地址複製貼上到顯示名稱的 [收件者] 欄位時，電子郵件地址不一定可被正確分析，並導致出現了一個顯示電子郵件地址無效的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-330">When a user copy-and-pastes an email address into the recipient field with the display name, the email address wasn't always parsed correctly and caused a warning about an invalid email address to appear.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-331">已修正此問題，可正確分析名稱和電子郵件地址，因此不會再顯示警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-331">It's been fixed so the name and email address are parsed correctly so the warning is no longer shown.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-332">我們修正了線上共用資料夾未傳回母資料夾名稱的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-332">We fixed an issue where online shared folders did not return parent folder name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-333">它並非失敗，而是傳回了不正確地移至主要帳戶的空白路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-333">Intsead of failing, it returned an empty path which incorrectly went to the primary account.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-334">我們修正了傳統附件無法使用 [另存為] 選項的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-334">We fixed an issue where the Save As option was not available for classic attachments.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-335">我們修正了讓使用者能在覆寫原則時自訂調整文字的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-335">We fixed an issue to provide a user a way to customize justification text when overriding a policy.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-336">我們已修正從唯讀預覽窗格中重新開啟 [草稿] 之後會開啟 [追蹤修訂] 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-336">We fixed an issue where track changes turned on after reopening draft from read-only preview pane.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-337">我們已修正關閉 [焦點收件匣] 並執行排序之後，電子郵件遭隱藏的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-337">We fixed an issue with emails being hidden after turning Focused Inbox off and doing a sort.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-338">我們已修正導致 Outlook 為啟用雲端設定的使用者建立第二個空白簽名的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-338">We fixed an issue that caused Outlook to create a second empty signature for people who had cloud settings enabled.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-339">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-339">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-340">我們修正了 PowerPoint 在匯出為 PDF 時，無法匯出矩形專案符號的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-340">We fixed an issue where PowerPoint was not exporting rectangle bullet points while exporting to PDF.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-341">我們已修正 GIF 在編輯器和投影片放映中的動畫只會執行一次的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-341">We fixed an issue where GIF's would animate only once in the editor and slide shows.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-342">我們已修正當使用者將來源路徑變更為本機 OneDrive 資料夾時，連結的 Excel 圖表不正確變更為 Excel 工作表的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-342">We fixed an issue where linked excel chart incorrectly changes to excel sheet when user changes the source path to local OneDrive folder.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-343">我們修正了若您在最後一張投影片上，且您在按 [結束工作模式] 之後和顯示摘要之前，滑向下一張投影片，則會在 [摘要] 頁面上看到 [結束工作模式] 對話方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-343">We fixed an issue that If you are on the last slide and if you swipe to the next slide after pressing 'End Session' and before the summary shows up, the End-Session dialog is visible on the summary page as well.</span></span>


### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-344">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-344">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-345">修正了如果您嘗試多次新增同一專案，且將 AttachToSources 設定為 false 時，ConsolidateProjects VBA 方法可能會發生出錯的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-345">Fixed an issue where the ConsolidateProjects VBA method may file if you try to add the same project multiple times and have AttachToSources set to false.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-346">已修正若您的事件程式碼執行中，並嘗試透過工作 [表單檢視] 進行變更，按一下 [確定] 按鈕可能不會提交變更的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-346">Fixed an issue where if you have eventing code running and try to make changes through a Task Form view, clicking the OK button may not commit the changes.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-347">修正了如果您嘗試多次新增同一專案，且將 AttachToSources 設定為 false 時，ConsolidateProjects VBA 方法可能會發生出錯的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-347">Fixed an issue where the ConsolidateProjects VBA method may file if you try to add the same project multiple times and have AttachToSources set to false.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-348">修正了如果您的自訂欄位包含公式，且正在使用實獲值分析，您可能會發現效能延遲切換檢視並開啟專案/工作詳細資料的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-348">Fixed an issue where if you have custom fields with formulas and are using earned value, you may notice performance delays switching views and opening project/task details.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-349">修正了如果您將群組套用到 [資源使用狀況] 或 [工作表] 視圖，然後插入欄位，Project 可能會當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-349">Fixed an issue where Project may crash if you apply a group by to the Resource Usage or Sheet view and then insert a column.</span></span>


### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-350">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-350">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-351">我們己修正已啟用工作流程檔案的連結無法如預期開啟的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-351">We fixed an issue where links to workflow enabled files were not opening as expected.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-352">修正當使用者在點擊追蹤的變更（插入/刪除）時，會彈出註解的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-352">Fixed an issue where a user tapping on a tracked change (insertion/deletion) would bring up a comment pop-out.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-353">我們已修正 Word 中刪除註解圖說文字的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-353">We fixed an issue with deleting comment callouts in Word.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-354">我們已修正 Outlook 有關將郵件設定為 [不要轉寄] 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-354">We fixed an issue with Outlook with message set to Do not forward.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-355">我們已修正有關儲存含有引文和方程式的 Word 文件問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-355">We fixed an issue with saving Word document that contains citation and equation.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-356">我們修正了 [樣式圖庫] 對話方塊的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-356">We fixed an issue with Style Gallery dialog.</span></span>


### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-357">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-357">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-358">當使用者從 Office 噴墨印表機上列印任何文件/檔案且列印機墨水不足時，即使噴墨印表機沒有碳粉，也會顯示「碳粉不足」或「無碳粉」消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-358">When the user prints any document/file on inkjet printers from Office and printer's ink is low, "Toner Low" or "No Toner" message will show, even though inkjet printers don't have toners.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-359">將訊息變更為顯示「碳粉/墨水不足」和「沒有碳粉/墨水」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-359">Changing message to display "Toner/ink Low" & "No toner/ink".</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-372">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-372">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-373">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-373">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-374">解决了搜尋未緩存共用行事曆時導致搜尋不傳回結果的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-374">Addresses an issue that caused Search to return no results when searching uncached shared calendars.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-375">解決了導致某些使用者觀察到在離線狀態下意外啟動 Outlook 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-375">Addresses an issue that caused some users to observe Outlook unexpectedly starting in an offline state.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-376">解決了導致代理人在開啟另一個信箱中的共用資料夾時出現錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-376">Addresses an issue that caused delegates to see intermittent failures when opening shared folders in another mailbox.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-377">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-377">PowerPoint</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-379">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-379">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-380">當使用者從 Office 噴墨印表機上列印任何文件/檔案且列印機墨水不足時，即使噴墨印表機沒有碳粉，也會顯示「碳粉不足」或「無碳粉」消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-380">When the user prints any document/file on inkjet printers from Office and printer's ink is low, "Toner Low" or "No Toner" message will show, even though inkjet printers don't have toners.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-381">將訊息變更為顯示「碳粉/墨水不足」和「沒有碳粉/墨水」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-381">Changing message to display "Toner/ink Low" & "No toner/ink".</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-459">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-459">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-460">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-460">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-461">此問題現在已解決，您不應該會再遇到當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-461">This issue has now been resolved and you should no longer experience a crash.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-462">我們已修正 ODBC 資料庫的連線對協力廠商應用程式沒有作用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-462">We fixed an issue where connections to an ODBC database were not working with third party applications.</span></span>


### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-463">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-463">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-464">我們修正了一個問題, 即如果您開啟包含LET 函數的檔案，它會顯示警示：”我們在您的檔案.xlsx 中發現內容有問題”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-464">We fixed an issue where if you opened a file containing the LET function, it would display the alert:  "We found a problem with content in "your file.xlsx".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-465">您想要我們儘量嘗試復原嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-465">Do you want us to try to recover as much as we can?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-466">如果您信任這個活頁簿的來源，請按一下 [是]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-466">If you trust the source of this workbook, click Yes".</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-467">我們修復了如果用戶鍵入包含括號的公式名稱並通過F1調用了協助，則該特定於公式的說明主題將不會顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-467">We fixed an issue where if a user typed a formula name including the parenthesis and invoked help via F1, the help topic specific to that formula would not be displayed.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-468">我們已修正使用巨集來設定某個範圍的 FormulaR1C1 屬性時，如果圖表工作表為作用中工作表，則儲存格參考會不正確的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-468">We fixed an issue where using a macro to set the FormulaR1C1 property for a range, the cell references would be incorrect if a chart sheet was the active sheet.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-469">我們修正了使用者無法修改樞紐分析表篩選的問題，因為它已設定為Analysis Services數據庫中不再存在的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-469">We fixed an issue where users could not modify a PivotTable filter because it was set to a value that was no longer present in an Analysis Services database.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-470">修正與 XLAM 增益集參照和具名範圍相關的損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-470">Fixed a crash related to XLAM add-in references and named ranges.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-471">我們修正了一個問題: 如果使用者將自訂樣式套用至動態陣列, 他們則會收到錯誤提示：「您無法變更陣列的一部分」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-471">We fixed an issue where if a user applied a custom style to a dynamic array, they would get the error: "You can't change part of an array".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-472">這是舊版限制，已移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-472">This was a legacy restriction that has been removed.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-473">修正在還原檔案的舊版本後，指派給按鈕的巨集會中斷的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-473">Fixed an issue where macros assigned to buttons were broken after restoring an older version of the file.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-474">我們已修正筆跡會導致 Excel 無法回應的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-474">We fixed an issue where inking could cause Excel to become unresponsive.</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-475">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-475">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-476">我們修正了一個問題, 讓您可透過群組政策來啟用/停用預設的登入選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-476">We fixed an issue which provides more flexibility in enabling / disabling the default logging options via Group Policy.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-477">我們修正了電子郵件草稿在助理和經理權限移動時, 寄件者的舊網域名稱仍被保留和顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-477">We fixed an issue where the Legacy Domain Name for an email sender was preserved and displayed after a draft of the email was moved between mailboxes with assistant permissions and manager permissions.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-478">修正會導致某些使用者看到 Outlook 在離線狀態中啟動，直到他們手動選擇線上工作為止的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-478">Fixes an issue that caused some users to see Outlook to start in an Offline state until they manually chose to work online.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-479">我們已修正在啟用單行功能區（SLR）後，執行 VBA 程式碼 ActiveInspector （"ShowSchedulingPage"）會導致執行階段錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-479">We fixed an issue where running the VBA code ActiveInspector.CommandBars.ExecuteMso("ShowSchedulingPage") after enabling the Single Line Ribbon (SLR) would result in a runtime error.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-480">我們修正了一個問題, 即Automatic Replies自動回復對話方塊上的確定和取消按鈕以高解析度（例如 1750 x 1920）及較大文字（例如175%）顯示的系統上的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-480">We fixed an issue where the 'OK' and 'Cancel' buttons on the Automatic Replies dialog would not be visible on a system with a high resolution (such as 1750 x 1920) combined with a large text size (such as 175%).</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-481">我們修正一個情況, 即將會議請求從空的聯繫人群組發送到另一個聯繫人組會導致當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-481">We fixed a condition where sending a meeting request from an empty contact group to another contact group would result in a crash.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-482">解決會導致使用者在開啟某些很大型電子郵件時會發生當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-482">Fixes an issue that caused users to experience a crash when opening certain very large emails.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-483">我們修正了一個問題, 它使的群組政策要求始終啟用增益集, 則 監視增益集的功能則無法使用，以防止使用者禁用增益集,。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-483">We fixed an issue where if Group Policy requires an Add-in to be always enabled, then monitoring add-in's becomes unavailable in order to prevent users from disabling the Add-in.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-484">解決一個問題，該問題導致使用者在選擇多個訊息時，能夠傳送 OneNote 所套用的「不可轉寄」原則的電子郵件內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-484">Addresses an issue that caused users to be able to send email content that had a "Do Not Forward" policy applied to OneNote when selecting more than one message.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-485">我們已修正一個問題，使用者現在可以停用 Outlook 的 IRM (資訊版權管理)，而不需要為其餘 Office 應用程式停用它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-485">We fixed an issue where users can now disable IRM (Information Rights Management) for Outlook without having to disable it for the rest of the Office applications.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-486">我們修正了 Active Directory 中的 "otherTelephone" 和 "otherHomePhone" 使用者帳戶屬性未對應到對應的 Outlook LDAP 屬性的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-486">We fixed an issue where the user account attributes in Active Directory for "otherTelephone" and "otherHomePhone" were not mapped to the corresponding Outlook LDAP attributes.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-487">此變更解決了在用戶將索引標籤從會議頁面切換到排程小幫手頁面後，會議頁面將繼續顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-487">This change fixes an issue where the Meeting page would continue to be displayed after the user switched tabs from the Meeting page to the Scheduling Assistant page.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-503">我們已修正刪除註解之後 Word 可能會當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-503">We fixed an issue where Word could crash after comments were deleted.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-504">我們修復了一個問題，即如果使用者建立的評論草稿, 錨定在已包含提交的評論行上，則在SideTrack與提交評論相關的草案則以錯誤的順序排列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-504">We fixed an issue where if a user created a comment draft anchored to a line already containing committed comments, then the draft was arranged in the wrong order relative to the committed comment in the SideTrack.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-505">我們修正了一個問題, 即如將文件縮放到160％或更高, 且註解窗格不可見，焦點將不會移至註解窗格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-505">We fixed an issue where the focus would not go to the comment pane if the document was zoomed to 160% or more and the comment pane was not visible.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-506">我們已修正一個問題，該問題造成使用者無法看到超出邊界的註解，因為在邊界中無法下拉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-506">We fixed an issue that prevented users from seeing comment threads that exceeded the sidetrack boundary because scrolling through the sidetrack was not working.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-507">我們修正了在邊界窗格中，搜尋已解決的註解無法正常運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-507">We fixed an issue where searching for resolved comments in the sidetrack pane was not working.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-508">我們修復了一個問題，即在多個打開的文件之間切換後，一個文件的註解會顯示在其他打開的文檔上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-508">We fixed an issue where the comments on one document would be displayed on other open documents after switching between the multiple open documents.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-509">我們已修正將文件儲存成 HTML 格式時，長連結無法換行的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-509">We fixed an issue where long links were not being wrapped when saving document to HTML format.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-510">我們已修正在某些情況下，項目符號無法在電子郵件中正確顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-510">We fixed an issue where in some cases, bullets are not displaying correctly in email.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-511">我們已修正 AutoOpen 會在 AutoExec 之前執行的巨集問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-511">We fixed an issue with macros in which AutoOpen runs before AutoExec.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-545">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-545">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-546">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-546">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-547">修正導致使用者嘗試從次要帳戶建立會議邀請的問題，讓帳戶新增至他們的個人檔案，而不會看到空白的表格: 是欄位而不是其電子郵件地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-547">Fixes an issue that caused users who attempted to create a meeting request from a secondary account added to their profile to not see a blank From: field instead of their email address.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-629">我們已修正具有放射狀漸層填滿的影像複本與原始不符的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-629">We fixed an issue where a copy of an image with a radial gradient fill did not match the original.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-630">我們修正了當應用程式視窗調整為小尺寸時，[搜尋] 編輯方塊中的預留位置文字發生溢出的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-630">We fixed an issue where the placeholder text in the Search edit box would overflow if the application window was resized to a small dimension.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-631">我們已修正如果新增註解來追蹤變更，將會意外開啟 [修訂] 窗格的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-631">We fixed an issue where if a comment was added to track a change, the revisions pane would unexpectedly open.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-632">我們修正了當焦點位於註解文字方塊中時，[編輯器] 命令會被停用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-632">We fixed an issue where the Editor command was disabled when the focus was in a comment text box.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-633">我們修正了當焦點位於註解文字方塊中時，[顯示標記] 命令會被停用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-633">We fixed an issue where the Show Markup command was disabled when the focus was in a comment text box.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-634">我們已修正刪除最後一個註解後，[新增批註] 按鈕停用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-634">We fixed an issue where the 'New comment' button would be disabled after deleting the last comment.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-635">我們已修正 [追蹤修訂] 中的 [特定人員] 選項已停用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-635">We fixed an issue where the 'Specific People' option for Track Changes was disabled.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-636">我們已修正文件連結未透過 [插入] > [連結] 下拉式功能表插入 [註解] 方塊的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-636">We fixed an issue where links to documents were not being inserted to the comments box via the Insert -> Link dropdown.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-637">我們已修正了開啟 HTML 檔案時偶爾停止回應的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-637">We fixed an occasional hang while opening HTML files.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-638">我們修正了自訂 XML 中的註解狀態在開啟文件時可能會遺失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-638">We fixed an issue in custom XML where the state of comments may be lost when opening the document.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-639">我們已修正 VBA 超連結集合中的超連結計數，在新增包含超連結的影像之後，未正確反覆運算的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-639">We fixed an issue where the hyperlink count in the VBA hyperlinks collection was not iterating correctly after adding an image containing a hyperlink.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-640">針對舊版非網頁服務的 [共用] 窗格，在開啟 [共用] 窗格下關閉文件時，可能會導致當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-640">For the old, non-web service based Share pane, upon closing the document while the Share pane is open could cause a crash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-641">這個問題現在已經修正。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-641">This is now fixed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-642">我們修正了使用者從工作列開啟新應用程式視窗，並建立新的空白檔時，會造成額外檔案建立的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-642">We fixed an issue where after the user opened a new app window from the taskbar and created a new blank document, additional files were created.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-643">我們修正了當使用者在編輯文件，但是許可權遺失時，我們並未通知使用者必須重新驗證的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-643">We fixed an issue where if a user was editing a document but had lost permissions, we were not notifying the user that they had to re-authenticate.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-697">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-697">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-698">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-698">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-699">我們已修正在重新整理連結的 SQL 資料表時，連結資料表管理員會提示您輸入主要索引鍵的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-699">We fixed an issue where the linked table manager would prompt a primary key if a linked SQL table was refreshed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-700">我們已修正 [查詢編輯器] 中的查詢捲出畫面的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-700">We fixed an issue where queries in the Query Editor scrolled out of view.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-701">我們已修正執行查詢的時間大約比預期完成時間兩倍久的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-701">We fixed an issue where query execution was taking approximately twice as long to complete than expected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-702">我們已修正導致 Microsoft Access 無法識別連結的 SQL Server 資料表中的識別資料行的問題，這可能會導致不正確地將資料列報告為已刪除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-702">We fixed an issue that caused Microsoft Access to fail to identify an Identity Column in a linked SQL Server table, which could cause rows to be reported as deleted incorrectly.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-703">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-703">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-704">我們已修正非 HTTP 或 HTTPS 型 URL 未顯示在 [最近用過的] 清單中的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-704">We fixed an issue where URLs that were not http or https based were not being displayed in the Most Recently Used list.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-705">已修正在載入含有多張分頁預覽的活頁簿時，可能會發生錯誤或當機問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-705">Fixed an issue where an error or hang may occur when loading a workbook with with multiple sheets in page break preview.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-706">我們修正以下問題：在特定版本 Excel 中建立的資料模型表格無法在 [表格預覽] 中看到，即使與該表相關聯的查詢尚未編輯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-706">We fixed an issue where data model tables created in certain versions of Excel could not be seen in 'Table Preview' even though the query associated with the table had not been edited.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-707">在 [定義名稱\套用名稱] 對話方塊中停用 [忽略相對/絕對] 參照會導致公式無法使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-707">Ignore Relative/Absolute' references in the Define Name \ Apply Names dialog would cause formulas to not work.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-708">我們已修正將活頁簿儲存至 SharePoint/OneDrive 時，會導致自訂功能區索引標籤 CustomUI XML 遭移除的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-708">We fixed an issue where CustomUI XML for a custom ribbon tab was removed when saving a workbook to SharePoint/OneDrive.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-709">我們已修正當建議以唯讀方式使用檔案時，活頁簿處於唯讀狀態的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-709">We fixed an issue where workbooks were read-only when the file only had read-only recommended.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-710">已修正在載入含有多張分頁預覽的活頁簿時，可能會發生錯誤或當機問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-710">Fixed an issue where an error or hang may occur when loading a workbook with with multiple sheets in page break preview.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-711">我們已修正雷達圖的主要格線無法正確設定格式的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-711">We fixed an issue where the major gridlines of radar charts could not be formatted correctly.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-712">我們已修正清除 [進階資料篩選] 可能會遺失表格格式設定的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-712">We fixed an issue where clearing an advanced data filter could lose table formatting.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-713">我們已修正嵌入式 PDF 文件的完整路徑顯示在文件標題，而不只是檔案名稱的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-713">We fixed an issue where the full path of an embedded PDF document would show in the document caption rather than just the filename.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-714">我們已修正停用 Wolfram 雲端連接器之後，儲存並重新開啟 Excel 活頁簿可能會導致當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-714">We fixed an issue where after disabling the Wolfram cloud connector and then saving and re-opening an Excel workbook, could result in a crash.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-715">我們已修正啟動 Excel 時啟用 [規劃求解] 增益集將導致當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-715">We fixed an issue where booting Excel with the Solver add-in enabled would result in a crash.</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-716">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-716">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-717">我們已修正如果在 [收件者] 行上有超過 130 個收件者，Outlook 會當機的問題，且我們也改善了呈現文字的效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-717">We fixed an issue where Outlook would hang if there were over 130 recipients on the 'To' line and we also improved the performance of rendering the text.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-718">我們已修正以下問題：當使用多個不同解析度的監視器時，輸入法編輯器 (IEM) 視窗會覆蓋透過 IME 輸入的文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-718">We fixed an issue where the Input Method Editor (IME) window would overlap the underlying text being entered via the IME when using multiple monitors with different resolutions.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-719">我們已修正「待辦事項列」中跨越兩天以上的活動，在後續的所有日期中顯示相同結束時間的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-719">We fixed an issue in the 'To Do Bar' where events that spanned more than two days, displayed the same end time for all subsequent days.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-720">解決會導致使用者看到他們透過拖放附件，以複製到其檔案系統所建立附件的建立日期設為 4501 年 1 月 1 日的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-720">Addresses an issue that caused users to see the creation date of attachments that they copied to their file system via drag and drop getting set to January 1, 4501.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-721">我們已修正使用者無法使用通訊群組清單中的「傳送為」或「代理傳送者」的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-721">We fixed an issue where users were unable to 'Send As' or 'Send on behalf' of a distribution list.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-722">解決在編輯經理行事曆上的現有行事曆約會時，導致代理人收到錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-722">Addresses an issue that caused delegates to receive an error when editing an existing calendar appointment on a manager's calendar.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-723">我們已修正導致使用者在關閉先前儲存的約會時看到下列錯誤的問題：「項目無法儲存，因為已被其他使用者或已在其他視窗中變更過。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-723">We fixed an issue that caused users to see the following error when closing an appointment that was previously saved "The item cannot be saved because it was changed by another user or in another window.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-724">您要在預設資料夾為這個項目建立複本?」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-724">Do you want to make a copy in the default folder for the item?"</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-725">解決會導致若「未」核取 [下載共用資料夾]，共用行事曆會議的 [回應選項] 中會遺失 [允許轉寄] 選項的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-725">Addresses an issue that caused the "Allow Forwarding" option to be missing from shared calendar meeting "Response Options" when Download Shared folder was NOT checked.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-726">解決選取安全性對話方塊上的 [儲存] 選項時，會導致使用者無法將來自其租用戶外部的 OneDrive 附件儲存至其本機電腦的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-726">Addresses an issue that caused users to be unable to save OneDrive attachments from outside their tenant to their local computer when selecting the "Save" option on the security dialog.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-727">我們已修正導致 Outlook 使用者在使用共用行事曆後，在幾分鐘內訊息清單停止更新的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-727">We fixed an issue that caused users of Outlook to see their message list stop updating for several minutes after using shared calendars.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-728">我們已修正行事曆提醒無法針對一週內即將到來的會議顯示確切時間的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-728">We fixed an issue that prevented calendar reminders from showing exact times for meetings coming up in less than a week.</span></span> 


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-729">我們已修正在郵件中插入影像內嵌，然後將郵件儲存為草稿將會重新調整影像大小的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-729">We fixed an issue where inserting an image inline in a message, then saving the message as a draft would result in a resizing of the image.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-730">我們已修正在編輯主旨之後，導致 NDR 郵件的本文從 Unicode 變更為 ASCII 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-730">We fixed an issue that caused the body of an NDR message to change from Unicode to ASCII after editing the subject.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-731">我們已修正迷你行事曆中的日期無法針對日本使用者顯示粗體的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-731">We fixed an issue where dates in the mini calendar failed to display in bold for users in Japan.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-732">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-732">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-733">我們已修正在即時共同撰寫工作階段期間，使用者的目前狀態色彩指示器無法在共同撰寫文件庫中重新整理的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-733">We fixed an issue where a user's presence color indicator was not getting refreshed in the co-authoring gallery during a live co-authoring session.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-734">我們已修正將 HTML 貼到投影片上的文字區域時，會改為貼上投影片最上方所建立的文字方塊中的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-734">We fixed an issue where pasting HTML to a text area on a slide would instead get pasted into a text box created at the top of the slide.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-735">我們已修正在 [簡報者檢視畫面] 中選取所有投影片、使用 Alt+Tab 退出 [簡報者檢視畫面] 並返回投影片放映，然後按一下 [結束放映] 時，將導致未處理例外狀況的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-735">We fixed an issue where selecting all slides in Presenter View, then exiting Presenter View using Alt+Tab and returning to the slide show and clicking 'End Show' would result in an unhandled exception.</span></span>


### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-736">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-736">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-737">已修正無法將從 Project 將 PDF/XPS 儲存至 SharePoint 文件庫的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-737">Fixed an issue where you couldn't save a PDF/XPS from Project to a SharePoint document library.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-738">修正 URL 以 .com 結尾時，無法從 Project Web App 在 Project 傳統型用戶端開啟專案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-738">Fixed an issue where projects couldn't be opened in the Project desktop client from Project Web App if the URL ended in .com.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-739">我們已修正 Project 在開啟特定 XML 檔案時可能當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-739">We fixed an issue where Project may crash when opening certain XML files.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-740">我們已修正 URL 以 '.com' 結尾時，無法從 Project Web App 在 Project 傳統型用戶端開啟專案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-740">We fixed an issue where projects couldn't be opened in the Project desktop client from the Project Web App if the URL ended in '.com'.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-741">已修正問題：如果您貼上具有多個相關性的工作，並不會正確複製所有相關性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-741">Fixed an issue where if you paste a task that has multiple dependencies, not all dependencies are copied correctly.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-742">已修正 [指派資源] 對話方塊中選取的工作與工作面板檢視中所選工作不同的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-742">Fixed an issue where the task selected in the assign resources dialog isn't the same as the task selected in the task board view.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-743">我們已修正當專案摘要工作，或專案 [開始/工作] 欄位變更時，ProjectBeforeTaskChange 事件無法觸發的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-743">We fixed an issue where the ProjectBeforeTaskChange event didn't fire when there was a change to the project summary task, either the project start/task field.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-744">我們已修正以下問題：如果固定工期的任務已 100% 完成，但未指定 [實際完成日期]，則任務的完成 % 將顯示為低於 100%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-744">We fixed an issue where if Fixed Duration tasks are at 100% complete but the Actual Finish is not specified, the Task % Complete would display as less than 100%.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-745">我們已修正以下問題：比較基準重設或更新可能會變更時間分段預算成本/工時資源，且比較基準反映不正確的預算值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-745">We fixed an issue where a baseline reset or update could change time-phased budget cost/work resources and the baseline could reflect incorrect budget values.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-746">我們已修正政府社群雲端中的 Project Planner 連結已停用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-746">We fixed an issue where Project Planner links in Government Community Cloud environments had been disabled.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-747">我們已修正如果文件庫處於新式模式，您無法從 SharePoint 文件庫開啟 Project 檔案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-747">We fixed an issue where you couldn't open a Project file from a SharePoint document library if the library was in modern mode.</span></span>


### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-748">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-748">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-749">我們已修正使用 Office 功能區中的 [清除格式設定] 按鈕清除 [註解] 窗格中的格式設定時，無法運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-749">We fixed an issue where the ability to clear formatting within the Comments pane via the Clear Formatting button in the Office Ribbon was not working.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-750">我們已修正將插入可縮放向量圖形 (SVG) 中的文字插入到 Word、Excel 或 PowerPoint 檔案、儲存並關閉檔案，然後重新開啟檔案後，難以辨識的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-750">We fixed an issue where text inserted in a Scalable Vector Graphic (SVG) was illegible after inserting it in a Word, Excel, or PowerPoint file, saving and closing the file, and then re-opening the file.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-751">我們已修正當尺規未顯示時變更表格大小，導致在背景中執行其他應用程式開始閃爍的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-751">We fixed an issue where changing the size of a table when the ruler is not displayed caused other applications running in the background to start flashing.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-752">我們已修正在共同撰寫模式中，註解回覆有時候不會顯示在 [註解] 窗格中，而是顯示在 [修訂] 窗格中的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-752">We fixed an issue where in co-authoring mode, comment replies would sometimes not show up in the comments pane but would be visible in the revisions pane.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-753">我們已修正在共同撰寫模式期間，當發生合併衝突且使用者已選取放棄變更時，我們不再顯示儲存或捨棄變更選項的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-753">We fixed an issue during co-authoring mode when there is a merge conflict and the user has already chosen to discard changes, we no longer display the option to save or discard changes.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-754">我們已修正 HTML 超連結色彩無法正確呈現的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-754">We fixed an issue where the HTML hyperlink color was not being rendered correctly.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-755">我們已修正以下問題：如果 Word 經常開啟的文件清單多於 50 個，然後儲存並開啟文件後，即使該文件沒有進行任何修訂，也會顯示歷程記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-755">We fixed an issue where if Word had a list of more than 50 frequently opened documents, then after saving and opening a document, a revision history would be displayed even though no revisions were made to that document.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-756">我們已修正共同撰寫期間的自動儲存問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-756">We fixed in issue with autosave during coauthoring.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-757">我們已修正一個問題，當嘗試使用新名稱儲存包含巨集的檔案時，無論使用者輸入什麼名稱，都會導致該檔案以 .docx 副檔名和檔案名稱 'WRO0004.docx' 儲存，進而導致文件無法使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-757">We fixed an issue that, when attempting to save a file containing a macro under a new name, would cause it to be saved with a .docx extension and the filename 'WRO0004.docx', regardless of what the user entered, rendering the document unusable.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-785">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-785">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-786">解決了當選取安全性對話方塊上的 [儲存] 選項時，導致使用者無法將 OneDrive 外部的 OneDrive 附件儲存至他們的本機電腦的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-786">Addressed an issue that caused users to be unable to save OneDrive attachments from outside their tenant to their local computer when selecting the "Save" option on the security dialog.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-787">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-787">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-789">當您啟用增益集，而登錄 TabProcGrowth 值為 REG_SZ 類型且其值為 "0"時，辦公主機視窗會當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-789">he office host was crashing in windows, when an add-in is being activated while the registry TabProcGrowth value is REG_SZ type and with value "0".</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-790">這個登錄 TabProcGrowth 值可以在下列4個路徑中的任何一個中： HKEY_CURRENT_USER \Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main HKEY_CURRENT_USER \Software\Policies\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE \Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINER \Software\Policies\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main 此變更將修正此問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-790">That registry TabProcGrowth value can be under any one of 4 paths: HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Policies\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINER\Software\Policies\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main This change would fix this issue.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-850">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-850">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-851">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-851">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-852">我們修正了在使用 OneDrive 時，Excel 偶爾會關閉的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-852">We fixed an issue where Excel would occasionally shut down when engaging OneDrive.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-853">我們修正了圖表座標軸自訂值無法正確套用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-853">We fixed an issue where custom values on the chart axis would not get applied correctly.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-854">我們修正了包含多個含有定義名稱的公式會導致儲存檔案時間加長的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-854">We fixed an issue where worksheets containing multiple formulas with defined names was resulting in longer times when saving files.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-855">我們修正了導致印表機名稱在可用印表機清單中重複的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-855">We fixed an issue that caused printer names to be duplicated in the list of available printers.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-856">我們修正了在使用者刪除合併的欄時，造成執行時間增加的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-856">We fixed an issue that resulted in improved performance time for users when they deleted merged columns.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-857">我們修正了因為增益集是以字母順序裝載，而不是以使用者指定的順序載入，而造成出現「因為此活頁簿目前有他人進行參考，而無法關閉」的錯誤訊息的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-857">We fixed an issue where the error message “This workbook is currently referenced by another and cannot be closed” would appear because add-ins were being loaded in alphabetical order rather than in a user specified order.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-858">我們修正了管理 Excel 與部分協力廠商輔助技術應用程式之間的字型時發生記憶體損毀的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-858">We fixed an issue where memory was being corrupted when managing fonts between Excel and some third party assistive technology applications.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-859">我們修正了在相同活頁簿中按一下加上書簽的超連結會導致活頁簿隱藏的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-859">We fixed an issue where clicking a bookmarked hyperlink within the same workbook would cause the workbook to be hidden.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-860">我們已修正某些複製和貼上的圖表連結使用的是映射磁碟機位址，而不是通用位址的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-860">We fixed an issue where some copy and pasted chart links used mapped drive addresses rather than universal addresses.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-861">我們修正了當 Excel 視窗透過 Teams 共用時，使用 Ctrl + Shift + 方向鍵滑動後，Excel 可能會無法回應的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-861">We fixed an issue where Excel could become unresponsive after using Ctrl+Shift+Arrow keys to scroll when the Excel window was shared through Teams.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-862">我們修正了當增益集在工作表中詢問含有 noSelect 鎖定的圖形的主項目目時，Excel 會當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-862">We fixed an issue where Excel would crash when Add-ins ask for Host Items on worksheets that contain shapes with noSelect locks.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-863">解決了嘗試將樞紐分析表插入圖表時 Excel 可能會當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-863">Addressed an issue where Excel may crash when attempting to insert PivotTables into a chart sheet.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-864">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-864">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-865">我們已修正以下問題：當使用多個不同解析度的監視器時，輸入法編輯器 (IEM) 視窗會覆蓋透過 IME 輸入的文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-865">We fixed an issue where the IME (Input Method Editor) window would overlap the underlying text being entered via the IME when using multiple monitors with different resolutions.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-866">我們已修正在撰寫新電子郵件訊息時，檢視範本會導致當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-866">We fixed an issue where viewing a template when composing a new email message would result in a crash.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-867">我們已修正在 Outlook 版本 1911之後，使用者無法使用 Exchange 2010 公用資料夾的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-867">We fixed an issue where users were unable to Exchange 2010 public folders after Outlook version 1911.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-868">我們修正了 Office 功能區中群組行事曆分類按鈕已停用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-868">We fixed an issue where the Categorize button for group calendars in the Office Ribbon was disabled.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-869">解決了 Outlook 無法啟用 [資料遺失保護原則] 提示使用 M365 商務版進階方案並為此服務付款的的使用者之問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-869">Addressed an issue where Outlook failed to enable Data Loss Protection policy tips people for users who had paid for the service who are on M365 Business Plus plans.</span></span>

The Date/Time Extended data type has better precision.:** Introducing a new and improved data type.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-929">為加強與 SQL 的語法相容性，並提高包含日期和時間之記錄的詳細資料和層級，我們正在將 DateTime2 資料類型實施到 Access 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-929">To enhance syntax compatibility with SQL, and to increase accuracy and level of detail in records that include dates and times, we’re implementing the DateTime2 data type into Access.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-930">這個額外的日期與時間資料類型，將會包含更大的日期範圍（0001-01-01 到9999-12-31），具有更高的指定時間精準度(以納秒取代秒為單位)，讓您可以提供和執行計算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-930">This additional date & time data type will include a larger date range (0001-01-01 through 9999-12-31), with higher-specified time precision (nanoseconds, rather than seconds) that you will be able to provide and perform calculations on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-931">若要啟用，請選取 [新增欄位] > [日期與時間延長]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-931">To enable, select New field > Date & Time Extended.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="5bc52-932">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-932">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/708c32da-a052-4cc2-9850-9851042e0024)

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-961">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-961">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-962">當您啟用增益集，而登錄金鑰 HKEY_CURRENT_USER \Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth 被設為零時，辦公主機視窗會當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-962">The office host was crashing in windows, when an add-in is being activated while the registry key HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth is set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-963">這變更將修正此問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-963">This change would fix this issue.</span></span>
