### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-994">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-994">Resolved issues</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-995">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-995">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-996">已增加搭配圖表使用的 [自訂誤差線] 對話方塊上儲存格參照 [編輯] 控制項的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-996">Increased the size of the cell reference edit controls on the Custom Error Bars dialog used with charts.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-997">修正圖表資料表無法正確呈現日期座標軸中的值的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-997">Fixed an issue where chart data table could render values in a date axis incorrectly.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-998">修正使用 [頁面配置] 或 [分頁預覽] 之後無法停用分頁符號的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-998">Fixed an issue where page breaks could not be disabled after going into Page Layout or Page Break Preview.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-999">修正隱藏和取消隱藏具有系列資料的欄之後，圖表線條樣式可能會遺失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-999">Fixed an issue where chart line styles could be lost after hiding and unhiding columns with series data.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1000">已修正在已篩選清單中插入欄的時間會比預期更長的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1000">Fixed an issue where inserting a column in a filtered list would take longer than expected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1001">已修正列印時表單控制項的核取方塊縮放的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1001">Fixed a problem with the scaling of checkboxes in form controls when printed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1002">已修正當檔案路徑太長時，在檔案重新開啟之後外部連結會停止運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1002">Fixed an issue where the external link stops working after the file is reopened if the file path is too long.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1003">在 Excel 2016 中使用數位簽章所儲存的活頁簿，會在於目前版本的 Excel 中開啟時導致簽章失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1003">Workbooks saved with a digital signature in Excel 2016 could have the signature invalidated upon opening in the current version of Excel.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1004">在某些情況下，Application.Evaluate (VBA) 無法在使用者定義的函式中運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1004">Application.Evaluate (VBA) was not working for User-defined functions in some cases.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1005">在 Excel 2016 中使用數位簽章所儲存的活頁簿，會在於目前版本的 Excel 中開啟時導致簽章失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1005">Workbooks saved with a digital signature in Excel 2016 could have the signature invalidated upon opening in the current version of Excel.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1006">此變更會修正設定格式化的條件 (CF) 資訊無法正確儲存到 XLSB 檔案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1006">This change fixes an issue where conditional formatting (CF) information was not being saved to XLSB files correctly.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1007">這項變更修正了即使 LINEST 函式傳回正確的值，圖表趨勢線的 R 平方值 (在強制 y 截距的情況下) 仍然不正確的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1007">This change fixes an issue where the chart trendline R-Squared value (in the forced y-intercept case) was incorrect even though the LINEST function returns the correct value.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1008">此變更修正了自訂圖表趨勢線格式不一定會儲存的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1008">This change fixes an issue where customized chart trendline formatting was not always being saved.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1009">當您使用舊版的「共用活頁簿」模式，嘗試為活頁簿的新工作表列出變更時，就會發生當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1009">A crash could occur when trying to list changes on a new sheet for a workbook using legacy"Shared Workbook" mode.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1010">修正啟用 [負值以補色顯示] 選項後，可能無法儲存樞紐分析表中的自訂格式設定的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1010">Fixed the issue where custom formatting in Pivot charts may not be saved when the "Invert if negative" option was enabled.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1011">修正如果選取 [負值以補色顯示] 選項，可能無法儲存樞紐分析表中單一資料點的自訂格式設定的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1011">Fixed an issue where custom formatting for a single data point in a Pivot chart was not saved if the "Invert if negative" option was selected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1012">這項變更修正在 CSV 檔案中上傳 '@' 字元時，會導致將 '@' 字元之後的字串轉換成公式的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1012">This change fixes an issue where the '@' character uploaded in a CSV file, would result in the string after the '@' character to be converted to a formula.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1013">修正無法正確捨入 SEQUENCE 函數中十進位值的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1013">Fixed an issue where decimal values in the SEQUENCE function were not rounded correctly.</span></span>

### <a name="onenote"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1014">OneNote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1014">OneNote</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1015">修正將分行符號儲存為垂直 Tab 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1015">Fixed an issue where line breaks were being stored as vertical tabs.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1016">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1016">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1017">解決會導致使用者無法將個人連絡人群組新增為會議出席者的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1017">Addresses an issue that caused users to be unable to add a Personal Contact Group as a Meeting attendee.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1018">已修正 Office 功能區中群組行事曆分類按鈕已停用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1018">Fixed an issue where the categorize button for group calendars in the Office Ribbon was disabled.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1019">已解決在 Windows 更新後，開啟儲存在本機的 msg 或 .oft 檔案會導致 Outlook 當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1019">Addressed an issue that caused Outlook to crash when opening .msg or .oft files that were saved locally after a Windows update.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1020">已修正企業客戶沒有執行或無法使用群組資料夾的問題，該問題會導致 Outlook 顯示「沒有回應」的訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1020">Fixed an issue where enterprise customers with group folders not implemented or not working, would result in Outlook displaying a "not responding" message.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1021">已解決導致使用者在 Outlook 桌面用戶端中按一下非常長的安全連結時，由於截斷而無法載入的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1021">Addressed an issue that caused very long safelinks that users clicked on in the Outlook Desktop client to fail to load due to truncation.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1022">修正當與伺服器同步處理時，名稱中包含 DBCS (雙位元組字元集) 字元的 Outlook 資料夾會間斷消失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1022">Fixed an issue where Outlook folders with names containing DBCS (Double Byte Character Set) characters would intermittently disappear when synchronizing with the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1023">為此，必須為 Outlook 設定 IMAP 帳戶，並在地區設定設定為日文的系統上執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1023">For this to happen, Outlook had to be configured with an IMAP account and running on a system with the locale set to Japanese.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1024">已解決會導致為使用者主要信箱以外的信箱所建立的刪除規則變得無效的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1024">Addressed an issue that caused delete rules created for mailboxes other than the user's primary mailbox to become invalid.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1025">已解決在轉寄加密郵件時導致捨棄附件的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1025">Addressed an issue that caused attachments to get dropped when forwarding an encrypted message.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1026">已解決會導致還有 2 個月時間的會議，無法在排程小幫手中顯示會議主題的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1026">Addressed an issue that caused meetings that are more than 2 months away to fail to display a meeting subject in the Scheduling Assistant.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1027">已解決會導致使用者在轉寄大型 HTML 郵件時，看到郵件內文截斷的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1027">Addressed an issue that caused users to see message body truncation when forwarding large HTML messages.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1028">新增透過群組原則強制執行 S/MIME 預設登入設定的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1028">Added the ability to enforce S/MIME default signing configuration via group policy.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1029">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1029">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1030">已修正問題：如果使用者建立了註解，但未張貼就關閉 [註解] 窗格，然後開啟新視窗、瀏覽多張投影片並關閉視窗，最後再開啟原始簡報中的 [註解] 窗格，將導致無法使用草稿註解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1030">Fixed an issue where if a user created a comment without posting it and closed the Comments pane, then opened a new window, navigated through multiple slides and, closed the window, and finally re-opened the Comments pane in the original presentation, the draft comments would not be available.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1031">修正了將滑鼠游標移到星號 (\*) 符號，但不會顯示上一次更新文件的日期和使用者姓名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1031">Fixed an issue where hovering over the asterisk (\*) symbol did not display the user name and date of the last person to update the document.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1032">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1032">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1033">在表單檢視中編輯前置/後續任務資料時，會觸發額外的 ProjectBeforeTaskChange 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1033">When Predecessor/Successor data is edited within a Form view, an extra ProjectBeforeTaskChange event is fired.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1034">修正變更連結至 SharePoint 工作清單之專案的面板狀態欄位時，Project 可能當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1034">Fixed an issue where Project may crash when changing the board status field on a project that is connected to a SharePoint task list.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1035">修正儲存使用舊版 Project 建立的專案時，Project 可能當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1035">Fixed an issue where Project may crash when saving projects created with older versions of Project.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1036">已修正如果 Project 連線至 Project Web App，且小數分隔符號是逗號，當新增延遲時，TaskDependencies Add 方法會失敗的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1036">Fixed an issue where if Project is connected to Project Web App and the decimal separator is a comma, TaskDependencies Add method fails when Lag is added.</span></span>


### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1037">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1037">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1038">修正在 [共同作業] 模式時，在文件中插入註解並不總是成功的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1038">Fixed an issue where inserting comments on a document in collaboration mode would not always work.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1039">此變更修正在按一下 @ 提及時，[人員卡片] 會閃動的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1039">This change fixes an issue where the People card would flash if the @ mention was clicked.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1040">啟用「顯示書簽」選項卻不會顯示書簽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1040">Enabling the option "Show bookmarks" would not display bookmarks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1041">已修正這個問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1041">This has been fixed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1042">修正問題：關閉具有草稿註解的文件時，會在不儲存草稿註解的情況下，提示使用者是否要關閉文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1042">Fixed the issue where closing a document with draft comments would prompt the user if they wanted to close the document without saving the draft comments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1043">取消提示會關閉文件，而不是保持文件開啟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1043">Cancelling the prompt would close the document rather than leaving it open.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1044">我們修正了複製及貼上標題的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1044">We fixed an issue in copying and pasting headings.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1045">已修正翻譯已張貼註解將導致「插入已翻譯的文字失敗」錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1045">Fixed an issue where translating a posted comment would result in the error 'Inserting translated text failed'.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1046">此變更修正了下列問題：如果已啟用 [顯示功能變數代碼，而非其值] 選項，則含有超連結的文字可能不會顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1046">This change fixes an issue where text with hyperlinks may not display if the option: "Show field codes instead of their values" was enabled.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1047">在 Web 檢視/沉浸式閱讀器中，如果已在檢視中，按一下提示會捲動到最上方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1047">In Web View/Immersive reader, clicking on a hint would scroll to the top even though it was already in view.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1048">已修正這個問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1048">This has been fixed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1049">我們已修正一個問題，當嘗試使用新名稱儲存包含巨集的檔案時，無論使用者輸入什麼名稱，都會導致該檔案以.docx 副檔名和檔案名稱 WRO0004.docx 儲存，進而導致文件無法使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1049">We fixed an issue that, when attempting to save a file containing a macro under a new name, would cause it to be saved with .docx extension and the filename WRO0004.docx, regardless of what the user entered, rendering the document unusable.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1050">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1050">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1051">當使用者收到將他們移至 Teams Only 的原則時，他們仍然可以使用商務版 Skype Outlook 增益集來排程會議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1051">When a user is given a policy that moves them to Teams Only, they were still able to use the Skype for Business Outlook add-in to schedule meetings.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1052">在此更新之後，當客戶端讀取指示用戶為 Teams Only 的策略並進入僅限會議加入模式後，您將不再能用商務版 Skype 安排會議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1052">After this update, you will no longer be able to schedule Skype for Business meetings after the client reads the policy indicating the user is Teams Only, and enters meeting join only mode.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1053">此外，如果商務版 Skype Outlook 增益集發現商務版 Skype 用戶端處於 [僅限會議加入] 模式，就無法自行啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1053">Additionally the Skype for Business Outlook Add-in will not activate itself while starting up if it sees the Skype for Business client is in meeting join only mode.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1054">此更新解決了 Microsoft Office 中的一個問題：可能無法在執行時期正確找到 Visual Basic for Applications 專案，這些專案的參照預期透搜尋 PATH 環境變數指定的位置來找到，進而導致VBA 執行時期錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1054">This update fixes an issue in Microsoft Office where Visual Basic for Applications projects with references that are expected to be found by searching locations specified in the PATH environment variable may not be found properly at runtime, leading to VBA runtime errors.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1055">此更新修正了 Microsoft Office 中 Visual Basic for Applications 中的問題，其中特定 VBA 專案參考了程式庫名稱或程式庫路徑中有 DBCS 字元的程式碼程式庫，因而在載入時被 Office 應用程式視為損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1055">This update fixes an issue in Visual Basic for Applications in Microsoft Office where certain VBA projects that contain references to code libraries with DBCS characters in the library name or library path would be viewed by the Office application as corrupt on load.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1129">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1129">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1130">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1130">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1131">**Facebook 連接器支援即將結束：** 於 2020 年 4 月起，Excel 就不再支援使用 Facebook 連接器的外部資料連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1131">**Facebook connector support is ending:** Starting in April 2020, Excel will no longer support external data connections that use the Facebook connector.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1132">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1132">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1133">**在 Outlook 中撰寫郵件時有新的選項可停用 @ 提及建議：** 您是否覺得 @ 提及的選擇器很煩人，一點都不好用？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1133">**New option to disable @ mention suggestions when composing mail in Outlook:** Do you find the @ mention picker more annoying than useful?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1134">現在您可以視需要將其關閉了。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1134">Now you can turn it off if you prefer.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1135">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1135">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1136">**在簡報時同步處理變更：** 即使簡報處於投影片放映模式，仍可即時同步處理所做的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1136">**Synchronize changes while you are presenting:** Synchronize changes whenever they are made even when the presentation is in slide show mode.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1137">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1137">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1138">**標註私人複本：** 製作共用文件的私人複本，以建立只有您本人能夠看到的手寫筆記。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1138">**Annotate your private copy:** Create hand written notes for your eyes by making a private copy of a shared document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1139">若要開始使用，請移至 [檢視] > [建立私人複本]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1139">Go to View > Create a Private Copy to get started.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1142">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1142">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1143">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1143">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1144">修正工作窗格中表格的重新調整及重新整理問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1144">Fixed issues with resizing and refreshing tables in the task pane.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1145">修正國際版 Access 在使用者介面中顯示英文字串的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1145">Fixed an issue where international versions of Access were displaying English strings in the user interface.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1146">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1146">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1147">已修正在工作表上選取儲存格範圍會導致只選取單一儲存格的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1147">Fixed an issue where selecting a range of cells on a sheet would result in the selection of a single cell.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1148">在 Excel 2016 中使用數位簽章所儲存的活頁簿，會在於目前版本的 Excel 中開啟時導致簽章失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1148">Workbooks saved with a digital signature in Excel 2016 could have the signature invalidated upon opening in the current version of Excel.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1149">已修正在複製含有樞紐分析表的工作表後，會於某些情況下導致 Excel 當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1149">Fixed an issue which would cause Excel to crash in some cases after copying a sheet containing a PivotTable.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1150">在某些情況下，Application.Evaluate (VBA) 無法在使用者定義的函式中運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1150">Application.Evaluate (VBA) was not working for User-defined functions in some cases.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1151">修正使用者在以程式設計方式編輯大量儲存格範圍時可能遇到的效能問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1151">Fixed a performance issue that users may have experienced when programmatically editing a large range of cells.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1152">修正以日文環境開啟 CSV 檔案時發生的效能問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1152">Fixed a performance issue that occurred when opening csv files with Japanese environments.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1153">已修正插入使用者定義的圖表範本來作為預設值會導致其儲存為直條圖的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1153">Fixed an issue where inserting a user defined chart template as default would result in saving it as a column chart.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1154">已修正當基礎資料儲存格沒有標題時，圖表上的資料標籤會以空白顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1154">Fixed an issue where Data labels on charts would display as blank when the underlying data cells did not have a caption.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1155">已修正在為含有 X 軸範圍的圖表縮減大小時，可能會導致 Excel 停止回應的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1155">Fixed an issue which could cause Excel to stop responding when reducing the size of a chart with some x-axis ranges.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1156">已修正已啟用 R1C1 儲存格參照且正在共同撰寫/共用的 Excel 工作表，在將游標移到 [使用者目前狀態] 圖示上方時不會以 R1C1 模式顯示作用中儲存格的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1156">Fixed an issue where an Excel sheet with R1C1 cell referencing enabled and is being co-authored / shared, hovering over the user presence icon does not display the active cell reference in R1C1 mode.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1157">此變更解決了處理格式錯誤或無效通訊協定資訊影像時所導致的延遲問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1157">This change addresses delays when processing images with malformed or invalid protocol information.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1158">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1158">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1159">此變更解決了處理格式錯誤或無效通訊協定資訊影像時所導致的延遲問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1159">This change addresses delays when processing images with malformed or invalid protocol information.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1160">此變更修正了電子郵件草稿最新變更未更新的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1160">This change fixes an issue where the latest changes to draft emails were not being updated.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1161">已修正在檔案上按一下滑鼠右鍵並使用「傳送到」功能無法運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1161">Fixed an issue where right-mouse clicking on a file and using 'Send to' would not work.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1162">已解決會導致代理人在不同機器上所看到的共用信箱有不同資料夾階層的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1162">Addressed an issue that caused delegates to see different folder hierarchies on different machines for shared mailboxes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1163">已解決會導致類別有時候會從電子郵件訊息中消失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1163">Addressed an issue that caused categories to occasionally disappear from email messages.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1164">已解決在變更機器上的時區時，會導致某些提醒無法觸發的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1164">Addressed an issue that caused some reminders to fail to fire when changing the timezone on a machine.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1165">已解決在嘗試檢視組織表單的屬性時，會導致使用者遇到當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1165">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience a crash when attempting to view the properties of an Organizational Form.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1166">已修正如果使用者有自訂的 [通訊錄] 搜尋路徑，則 Outlook 的名稱解析範圍會限制為自訂路徑，而不是包括全域通訊清單 (GAL) 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1166">Fixed an issue where if a user had a customized the search path for the Address book, Outlook's name resolution scope would be limited to the customized path rather than including the Global Address List (GAL).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1167">解決了會讓 [附件工具] 中的 [儲存至雲端] 按鈕不見的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1167">Addressed an issue that caused the "Save to Cloud" button to be missing from Attachment Tools.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1168">解決了以下問題：當使用者從檢查程式視窗回覆受到數位版權管理的郵件，卻沒有所回覆郵件的擁有者權限時，使用者會無法新增簽名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1168">Addressed an issue that caused users to be unable to add a signature when replying to a digitally rights managed message from an inspector window when the user does not have Owner permission on the message being replied to.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1169">解決了以下問題：使用者無法從網頁位置將其他附件新增到先前建立的會議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1169">Addressed an issue that caused users to be unable to add additional attachments from a web location to a previously created meeting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1170">解決將附件新增至郵件或從郵件拖放 (與透過功能表相對) 來儲存附件時，導致檔案的「上次修改」日期更新的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1170">Addressed an issue that caused the "Last Modified" date on a file to be updated when adding an attachment to a mail or saving an attachment from a mail by dragging and dropping it (as opposed to via a menu).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1171">解決會導致在展開的尋找窗格中按一下 Enter 時無法開始搜尋，而是會要求使用者按一下 [搜尋] 按鈕的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1171">Addressed an issue that caused hitting enter in the expanded find pane to fail to start a search, requiring instead that users click on the search button.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1172">已修正在一組傳回的搜尋結果中，依類別結果排序不會顯示類別色彩的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1172">Fixed an issue where within a set of returned search results, sorting the results by Categories would not display the Category colors.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1173">修正將 [如果有，顯示使用者的照片] 選項停用時，搜尋不會顯示有關使用者的任何資訊的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1173">Fixed an issue where search shows no information about users when the option to "Show user photographs when available" is disabled.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1174">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1174">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1175">此變更修正了會導致包含 emojis 的 PowerPoint 檔案在儲存時發生失敗的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1175">This change fixes an error that could cause PowerPoint files containing emojis to fail when saving.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1176">此變更修正了在 PowerPoint 或 Word 中呈現內嵌為 OLE 物件的舊版 Excel 圖表時可能不會永遠顯示圖表標題的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1176">This change fixes an issue where the rendering of a legacy Excel chart embedded as an OLE object in PowerPoint or Word may not always display the chart title.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1177">我們已修正將文字從 Excel 複製到 PowerPoint 時可能會導致其格式設定發生變更的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1177">We have fixed an issue when copying text from Excel to PowerPoint might change its formatting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1178">此變更修正了使用 [全字拼寫須相符] 來尋找特殊字元時，不一定能正常運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1178">This change fixes an issue where finding special characters using 'find whole words only' did not always work as expected.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1179">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1179">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1180">修正無法正確計算摘要工作日期的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1180">Fixed an issue where summary task dates weren't always getting calculated correctly.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1181">修正不先執行 OpenUndoTransaction 方法就不能觸發 OnUndoOrRedo 事件的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1181">Fixed an issue where the OnUndoOrRedo event doesn't fire without first running the OpenUndoTransaction method.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1182">已修正當使用者按一下 [排程群組] 內 [工作] 功能區中的 [停用] 按鈕時，不會觸發 'ProjectBeforeTaskChange' Visual Basic Applications (VBA) 事件的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1182">Fixed an issue where the 'ProjectBeforeTaskChange' Visual Basic Applications (VBA) event did not fire when a user clicked the “Inactivate” button found on the Tasks Ribbon within the Scheduling grouping.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1183">如果您在 [表單類型] 檢視中設定前置任務或後置任務詳細資訊，則 ProjectBeforeTaskChange Visual Basic Applications (VBA) 事件不會一律擷取變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1183">If you set predecessor or successor details from within a Form type view, the ProjectBeforeTaskChange Visual Basic Applications (VBA) event didn't always capture the changes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1184">例如，如果刪除了某個相依性，並在表單上按一下 [確定]，則不會觸發該事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1184">For example, if you deleted a dependency and clicked OK on the form, the event did not fire.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1185">已修正此問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1185">This behavior has been fixed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1186">已修正在進行變更 (例如日期變更) 之後，實際工作成本 (ACWP) 的最新值不會顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1186">Fixed an issue where the latest values for the Actual Cost of Work Performed (ACWP) would not be displayed after making a change, such as a date change.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1187">已修正使用「最近使用」(MRU) 功能表開啟專案時，會使用 [讀取/寫入] 存取權開啟專案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1187">Fixed an issue where opening a project using the Most Recently Used (MRU) menu opened the project file with Read/Write access.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1188">這項變更修正了如果您建立包含開始日期和時間 (但無工期) 的手動工作，則時間表上的時間顯示不正確的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1188">This change fixes an issue where if you created a manual task with a start date and a time (but no duration), it would be displayed with an incorrect time on the timeline.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1189">已修正使用回曆列印時間表時，會導致列印檢視中略過或重複一個月的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1189">Fixed an issue where printing a timeline using a Hijri calendar would result in a month being skipped or duplicated in the print view.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1190">這項變更解決了在團隊規劃中使用 GDI 物件時，可能導致 GDI 物件分配過多並產生記憶體不足的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1190">This change addresses an issue where working in Team Planner with GDI objects, could result in the over allocation of GDI objects and create low memory conditions.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1191">修正了以下問題：如果執行 'CustomFieldValueListGetItem' 且自訂欄位的查閱資料表不存在，系統會建立一個不應建立的空白查閱資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1191">Fixed an issue where if CustomFieldValueListGetItem' is executed and a lookup table for the custom field doesn't exist, an empty lookup table is created even though it should not be.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1192">在表單檢視中編輯前置/後續任務資料時，會觸發額外的 ProjectBeforeTaskChange 事件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1192">WhenPredecessor/Successor data is edited within a Form view, an extra ProjectBeforeTaskChange event is fired</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1193">修正了當開啟保護實際工作的設定時，使用者無法輸入分時期基準工時的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1193">Fixed an issue where the user couldn't enter time-phased Baseline Work when the setting to protect actual work is on.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1194">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1194">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1195">此變更修正了將游標懸停在提示上並不會醒目提示其卡片的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1195">This change fixes an issue where hovering a cursor over a hint would not highlight its card.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1196">此變更修正了以下問題：從 [檢視] 功能表選取多個頁面時，其中的 [註解] 窗格會顯示為空白。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1196">This change fixes an issue with multiple pages selected from the View menu, where the comments pane could be displayed as blank.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1197">已修正張貼留言功能停用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1197">Fixed an issue where the functionality to post comments was disabled.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1198">此變更修正了使用套索選取工具時，群組圖形中的文字會暫時消失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1198">This change fixes an issue that would cause the text in grouped shapes to disappear temporarily when using the Lasso selection tool.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1199">此變更解決了處理格式錯誤或無效通訊協定資訊影像時所導致的延遲問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1199">This change addresses delays when processing images with malformed or invalid protocol information.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1200">此變更修正了在 PowerPoint 或 Word 中呈現內嵌為 OLE 物件的舊版 Excel 圖表時可能不會永遠顯示圖表標題的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1200">This change fixes an issue where the rendering of a legacy Excel chart embedded as an OLE object in PowerPoint or Word may not always display the chart title.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1201">這項變更解決了帳戶管理員不會分派訊息而導致協力廠商應用程式懸置的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1201">This change addresses an issue where the account manager would not dispatch messages resulting in a hang with third party applications.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1202">此變更修正了在雙頁檢視中建立註解時，註解錨點不一定會顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1202">This change fixes an issue in two page view, when creating a comment, the comment anchor did not always come into view.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1203">修正輸入或編輯備註然後使用 Ctrl+A 時，會導致選取畫布中的文字，而不只是選取備註卡片內文字的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1203">Fixed an issue when typing or editing a comment and using Ctrl+A would result in selecting text in the canvas instead of selecting text just within the comment card.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1204">已修正如果段落的樣式是連結至清單的樣式上階，則該清單的編號可能會遺失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1204">Fixed an issue where if a paragraph whose style is an ancestor of a style linked to a list, then the numbering of that list could be lost.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1205">這項變更修正了目錄會使用文件中未包含的標題樣式進行更新的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1205">This change fixes an issue where the Table of Contents would get updated with heading styles which were not present in the document.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1206">我們已修正文件中的文字對齊，在使用 [快速列印] 進行列印之後嘗試進行編輯時變得混亂的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1206">We fixed an issue which alignment of word in document gets scrambled when tried to edit after printing using Quick Print.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1207">我們已修正將兩份文件合併成一份文件時的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1207">We fixed an issue when merging 2 documents into one document.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1208">已修正在寄送文件時，儲存在 Word 文件中的數位簽章會被刪除的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1208">Fixed an issue where digital signatures saved in Word documents would be removed when mailing the documents.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1209">修正標示的修訂若與方程式有關，在儲存檔案時可能會導致失敗的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1209">Fixed an issue where marking revisions involving equations could result in a failure when saving the file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1325">已修正當檔案中的第一個字為 TABLE 時，CSV 檔案載入錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1325">Fixed an issue where CSV files were loaded incorrectly when the first word in the file was TABLE.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1326">已修正當您在兩個具有不同縮放比例的活頁簿之間切換時，使用者可能遇到的當機問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1326">Fixed an issue where users may have experienced crashes when switching between two workbooks that had different zoom levels.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1328">此變更可解決物件模型中的執行階段錯誤，以及當增益集要求的文件/工作表上的主機項目包含具有 noSelect 鎖定的圖形時，應用程式 (Excel、Word) 的潛在當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1328">This change addresses a run-time error in the object model and potential crash of the App (Excel, Word) when Add-ins ask for Host Items on documents/worksheets that contain shapes with noSelect locks.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1329">解決導致 Outlook 使用者在同步處理設定時發生當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1329">Addresses an issue that caused Outlook users to experience a crash when synchronizing settings.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1366">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1366">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1370">修正 Word/Excel/PowerPoint 中的使用者主體名稱 (UPN) 不再區分大小寫，導致在 SharePoint 上使用檔案時較少發生失敗的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1370">Fixed an issue Word/Excel/PowerPoint where the User Principal Name (UPN) is no longer case sensitive resulting in less failures when working with files on SharePoint.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1371">修正在 Word/Excel/PowerPoint 中開啟來自相同 SharePoint 文件庫的多個文件時，僅掃描開啟的第一個文件是否符合原則的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1371">Fixed an issue when multiple documents are open in Word/Excel/PowerPoint from the same SharePoint library, only the first document opened will be scanned for Policy compliance.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1463">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1463">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1464">更新和瀏覽目錄時，有時可能會在文件上顯示灰色區域的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1464">Updating and scrolling through a table of contents may sometimes display a gray area over the document.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1465">修正在已撰寫註解但未張貼，且使用者嘗試儲存檔案的情況下，使用 [瀏覽] 來儲存檔案沒有作用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1465">Fixed an issue where using 'Browse' to save a file did not work if a comment was written but not posted and the user tried to save the file.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1466">已修正在註解卡片之間來回切換時，有時會顯示一開始選取的註解，並將某選取範圍醒目提示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1466">Fixed an issue where going back and forth between comment cards would sometimes display the initially selected comment with a selection highlight.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1467">已修正在編輯備註之後將文字設為斜體然後再張貼，斜體格式設定遺失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1467">Fixed an issue where italics formatting is lost after editing a comment, italicizing the text and then posting it.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1468">已修正在具有「反轉」頁面色彩的閱讀模式中，備註提示未顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1468">Fixed an issue where comment hint was not visible in read mode with Inverse page color.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1469">已修正共同撰寫文件時，可能不會保留根註解的草稿版本的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1469">Fixed an issue where if a document is being coauthored, the draft version of a root comment may not be preserved.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1470">將 SlideTrack 啟用且 [註解] 窗格關閉時，Ctrl+Alt+M 可能無法開啟 [註解] 窗格的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1470">With SlideTrack enabled and the comments pane closed, Ctrl+Alt+M may not open the comments pane.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1471">修正在表格中新增 @提及時可能發生錯誤訊息：「文件中的表格已經毀損」的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1471">Fixed an issue when adding @mention in a table could generate the error message: 'A table in this document has become corrupted'.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1472">修正備註內容功能表中的備註命令 (編輯備註、回覆備註、刪除備註、解決備註) 未顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1472">Fixed an issue where comment commands (Edit comment, Reply to comment, Delete comment, Resolve comment) in the comments context menu were not being displayed.</span></span>


### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1473">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1473">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1474">解決可能導致挪威耐諾斯克 (nn-no) 校訂工具套件安裝不正確的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1474">Resolves an issue that may have caused Norway Nynorsk (nn-no) proofing tools package to be installed incorrectly.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="5bc52-1475">此變更解決使用 Intel Integrated GPU 的圖形配接卡報告問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5bc52-1475">This change addresses reported problems with graphics adaptors that leverage the Intel Integrated GPU.</span></span>
